< review>
A wonderful rescue that truly cares about their dogs, and goes to great lengths to ensure that a pup is going into a good home. Yes, there are a few hoops to jump through (detailed application, home check, and an appointment must be made in order to meet dogs) but this is all for the sake of the dogs. My experience was extremely positive: My coordinator was very responsive (answered all questions I had before adopting, made recommendations of dogs that might be a good fit for me, and helped me with questions post-adoption, too), the process was streamlined, and I was truly impressed that The Barking Lot is able to accomplish so much with a 100% volunteer staff. Plus, they matched me up with the furry little love of my life, Scooter. I loved my experience so much that I became a volunteer for TBL, which has also been a truly rewarding experience.< /review>

< review>
We had a great experience with the Barking Lot. We submitted our application online, scheduled a home visit within a week, and went to meet dogs a couple days after that. The dog we originally had our eye on was being adopted when we arrived, so they listened to what we were looking for and introduced us to several other dogs who fit the bill. They give you as much time as you need with each dog and let you take them for a little walk to get to know them. We fell in love with one and picked her up the next day after she had been spayed. Every dog we met was healthy, happy, and well cared for. The volunteers clearly love the dogs and care deeply about matching them with great homes. As other reviews have mentioned, communication isn't always immediate, and it's not the most organized place on earth. I imagine this is because they are a donation-based, volunteer-run organization rescuing dogs from literally all over the world. They have a lot going on, and what they do is not easy. Be patient and follow their process, and you won't have any issues.< /review>

< text>
The Barking lot is a shelter that gets absolutely no county or city funds. We used to volunteer there and, yes it is a bit dirty and smelly because they don‚Äôt have the funds like the Humane Society or other county shelters. However, if you can get beyond these exteriors of abruptness, and appearance I‚Äôd the shelter, You can experience what we did: everyone at the Barking Lot, working and volunteering, has a very big and good heart.

Stacey saved our beautiful dog, Big Boy aka Biggy.  A beautiful, pure white, American Bulldog/pit bull mix.
He was dragged behind a car, had broken and missing teeth from being hit, and appeared he could have died from starvation alone. He had twine tucked deeply into his skin around his mouth so as not to eat.  Biggie was in line to be euthanized.  Stacey saved him.

And by doing this, the Barking Lot gave my family the most unbelievably warm, gentle, intuitive, and lovable dog I have ever had or seen in my life.  As our adopted 2 year old grew, who also had physical issues of her own, Big Boy and she became tightly bonded.  Big Boy has been the love of our lives, especially our daughter‚Äôs, who is now 6 years old.
Big Boy got cancer a few months ago in the leg that they dragged him by, and which he never recovered.  A few weeks ago, Big Boy passed away.  He hung on for all of us as we were all so close.  Prior to us knowing he had cancer, my husband ran into Stacey with Big Boy.  My husband said that Biggie immediately knew Stacey and gave her his gratitude, in his special way.

So, perhaps the Barking Lot smells, isn‚Äôt that clean, and I have also experienced a bit of abruptness by the staff. However,  when it comes to rescuing and saving thousands of dogs on small amount of funds, these folks know what they‚Äôre doing.  Please trust me. You may be missing the dog of your lifetime, as we had with Big Boy.

All my gratitude to the Barking Lot-
Dr. P. Sloane
La Jolla, ca</text>

We encourage people to bring cash and make an offer. No prices are set in stone so if you really did see something in our shop that was priced higher than online it's better to just bring it to our attention and make an offer.\n\nWe also know that the flip side of bringing an item in to sell or get a loan on can be a little vexatious for both customers and our staff as we go through the negotiation process.\nFirst and foremost customers can always expect us to be transparent and honest in our assessment of items and in our business practice.\nThat said sometimes with certain items we have a level of comfort and expertise as to what we are willing to invest and risk on particular items. These are challenging business decisions with a delicate balance between being fair and just and making sure that we can keep our business growing to help more members of the community.\n\nCertainly there are less expeditious ways to sell your items that may yield a more profitable transaction such as selling your items directly to another consumer who intends to use it themselves.\nIt's important to understand we are not consumers, we are brokers with cash on hand to make an immediate purchase on items for the opportunity to resell for a profit ourselves.\nOften people don't want to do the additional legwork or take the time to find another consumer so it's an easier faster process to sell it to a pawnshop.\n\nThis response is getting long but we do want to speak to your last point regarding percentages on loans. While your review doesn't speak to the item you attempted to get a loan on and since we do our best to maintain customer confidentially I will just speak in broad terms.\nWe loan on array of items, jewlery, musical instruments, coins, collectibles, tools, and even some electronics if they're in fantastic shape and still moderately new.\nCertain items like jewlery and collectibles typically maintain their value for a much longer period of time and are easily resold compared to electronics and inexpensive musical instruments which begin to depreciate immediately after their purchase at a retail store.\nIn California loans are good for 130 days. that's over four (4) months an item is just sitting in a pawnbrokers storage room depreciating. That said all pawnbrokers write loans on a sliding scale percentage based on the merits of the  item. I.e. type, condition, performance, upgrades, length of life, and perceived depreciation. We certainly take a look at customers who have established a solid reputation and rapport with us as well to try to help our customers meet their needs but in the end it's only an offer that one must agree to. Sometimes negotiations don't work out and we hope to shake hands and make a deal on a different item next time.\n\nI hope this clears things up for you and you will reconsider visiting our store with your newly furnished knowledge of how our pawn shop operates.\nIf not at least give us a wave as you drive by to your next review of a fast food joint or cheap motel."}<//Response>

<resp>None< /resp><text>COOLEST Panera Bread store I've ever experienced! I walked in and immediately fell in love with the space. It's got a warm industrial-modern feel with high ceilings, rustic wood tables and exposed brick walls. I'm so excited that we now have a store in Beverly Hills. The Hot Turkey Panini w/ a cup of Tomato soup is my all-time favorite. Today I tried the LENTIL QUINOA BOWL WITH CHICKEN and it was DELICIOUS. It had fresh kale and spinach, quinoa and lentils, antibiotic-free chicken, all in a flavorful soy-miso broth. You have to try it!!!

Overall: There is such a unique vibe in the store that I've never experienced at any other Panera. Plus, the food is incredible. There's free wifi, staff is attentive yet knows when to leave you alone. I see it as a great working space to go/hang out on the computer writing and relaxing.

Loved it. Proud to be the first to share this awesome cafe with everyone on Yelp. So glad I finally have a Panera in Beverly Hills, Beverly blvd is now complete!< /text>< Time>

< text>
I can't rate their food because I can't eat what they gave me. But I can rate my experience.

I'm on a low carb diet, so I ordered a bowl w/chicken, cheese, lettuce, and sour cream to go. The guy taking my order offered guac, so I got that too.

Unfortunately, I ended up with a high-carb burrito with a ton of rice & beans and no guac. I didn't notice this until I got home and ended up just giving the burrito to someone who wasn't on a diet. Honestly, I know I should've gone back, but it was a long ride home and a long, tiring day at work.

I'll say that the food looks delicious and give them a benefit of a doubt. My friend enjoyed the tacos they got and I'm sure they'll enjoy the burrito as well. I'll try going back in another time, but I'm hoping to get the right order so I can give a higher rating.</text>

<Review>Ruth Hardy Park is a great park overall.  It offers a lot of space where one can engage in all types of activities.  Basketball, tennis courts, play ground, dog area, outdoor fitness machines (very basic) and several picnic tables with outdoor grills.  Plenty of parking. Large perimeter to walk.  Its not a loud park with cars pumping out loud music. Its kept very clean and tidy.   There is a larger elder community who enjoy this park.  Sometimes you'll see company picnics and the occasional flag football games being enjoyed.  There are a tiny bank of bleachers at the tennis courts. I do recommend this park for anyone who seeks a simple outdoor fix.</Review>< pics>
